\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
TI B\+Q2560x battery charge IC driver. 

Detail will be writen soon \begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
In order to use this driver the {\ttfamily U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+R\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+U\+LE} option must be enabled in {\ttfamily config.\+h}.
\end{DoxyPrecond}
\hypertarget{group___c_h_a_r_g_e_r_charger_1}{}\doxysubsection{Stateflow}\label{group___c_h_a_r_g_e_r_charger_1}
The driver implements a state machine internally, not all the driver functionalities can be used in any moment, any transition not explicitly shown in the following diagram has to be considered an error and shall be captured by an assertion (if enabled). 
\begin{DoxyImageNoCaption}
  \mbox{\includegraphics[width=\textwidth,height=\textheight/2,keepaspectratio=true]{dot_inline_dotgraph_3}}
\end{DoxyImageNoCaption}
